Great — now we do this properly step-by-step like a build guide, not theory. I’ll guide you from wiring → testing → full integration.

You have enough components to make a working smart medicine dispenser prototype 👍

🧩 SYSTEM OVERVIEW (what you’re building)
ESP32 (main brain) → controls everything

RTC (DS1307) → keeps time

Servo (SG90) → dispenses medicine

IR sensors → detect pill presence / user interaction

LCD (JHD162A + I2C) → show time + alerts

Buzzers + LEDs → alerts

Push buttons → manual control

⚠️ ESP32-CAM is optional for now → don’t use it yet
(We’ll add later if needed. First make core system work.)

🛠️ STEP 1: POWER SETUP (VERY IMPORTANT)
⚡ Use ESP32 as central power
Power ESP32 using Micro USB

Use ESP32 pins to power components:

ESP32 Pin	Use
3.3V	RTC, IR sensors
5V/VIN	LCD + Servo
GND	Common ground for ALL
⚠️ Rule: ALL GNDs must be connected together

🔌 STEP 2: RTC (DS1307) CONNECTION
👉 Use I2C communication

RTC Pin	ESP32 Pin
VCC	3.3V
GND	GND
SDA	GPIO 21
SCL	GPIO 22
✅ Put RTC on breadboard

📺 STEP 3: LCD (JHD162A + I2C adapter)
Your I2C adapter makes it EASY.

LCD I2C Pin	ESP32
VCC	5V
GND	GND
SDA	GPIO 21
SCL	GPIO 22
✅ Same SDA/SCL as RTC (shared bus)

🔁 STEP 4: SERVO MOTOR (SG90)
Servo Wire	ESP32
Red	5V
Brown	GND
Orange	GPIO 13
⚠️ Important:

Servo should be on breadboard power rail

If unstable → later use external power

👀 STEP 5: IR SENSORS (2 units)
IR Pin	ESP32
VCC	3.3V
GND	GND
OUT	GPIO 34 (IR1), GPIO 35 (IR2)
🔘 STEP 6: PUSH BUTTONS (2)
Use pull-down logic:

Button	ESP32
Button 1	GPIO 25
Button 2	GPIO 26
👉 Wiring:

One side → 3.3V

Other side → GPIO + 10k resistor to GND

(If confusing, I can draw it for you)

🔊 STEP 7: BUZZERS (2)
Buzzer	ESP32
+	GPIO 27 / GPIO 14
-	GND
💡 STEP 8: LEDs (3)
LED	ESP32
LED1	GPIO 18
LED2	GPIO 19
LED3	GPIO 23
👉 Add 220Ω resistor in series

🔧 STEP 9: BREADBOARD LAYOUT (IMPORTANT)
Layout idea:
Breadboard 1:

RTC

LCD I2C

IR sensors

Breadboard 2:

Servo

Buttons

LEDs + Buzzers

👉 Connect power rails across boards

🧪 STEP 10: TESTING ORDER (DON’T SKIP)
Test one-by-one:
✅ Blink LED

✅ LCD display “Hello”

✅ RTC time reading

✅ Servo rotate

✅ IR sensor detection

✅ Button press

✅ Buzzer sound

⚠️ NEVER connect everything at once initially

🧠 STEP 11: BASIC WORKING LOGIC
Your final flow:

RTC → checks time
IF time == medicine time:
    → buzzer ON
    → LED ON
    → LCD message
    → servo rotates (dispense)

IR sensor:
    → detect if medicine taken

Button:
    → manual dispense / stop alarm
⚠️ COMMON MISTAKES (avoid these)
❌ No common ground → nothing works
❌ Servo directly from weak supply → ESP resets
❌ Wrong SDA/SCL pins → LCD/RTC fail
❌ Connecting 5V to wrong pins → DAMAGE

🚀 WHAT NEXT
Next step I recommend:

👉 I give you:

Full Arduino code (ready to upload)

Proper circuit diagram (visual)

Then mobile app integration

Let’s focus clearly on LCD (JHD162A + I2C module) connection.

📺 🔌 HOW TO CONNECT LCD (WITH I2C ADAPTER)
🧩 What you actually have
Your LCD is:

JHD162A (16x2 display)

With I2C adapter (PCF8574 module) attached behind

👉 That means you ONLY need 4 wires (very easy)

🔌 CONNECTION TABLE
LCD (I2C) Pin	ESP32 Pin
VCC	5V
GND	GND
SDA	GPIO 21
SCL	GPIO 22
📍 VISUAL UNDERSTANDING

⚠️ IMPORTANT THINGS
1. Same pins as RTC
RTC and LCD both use:

SDA → GPIO 21

SCL → GPIO 22

👉 This is correct (I2C supports multiple devices)

2. Adjust contrast
On the I2C module there is a small blue potentiometer
👉 Rotate it with screwdriver until text becomes visible

3. Default I2C address
Usually:

0x27 OR 0x3F

We’ll confirm in code later

🧪 QUICK TEST CODE (VERY IMPORTANT)
Upload this to check LCD:

#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2); // try 0x3F if not working

void setup() {
  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();
  
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Hello Asmit!");
  
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("LCD Working");
}

void loop() {
}
❌ IF LCD NOT WORKING
Try these fixes:

🔁 Change address
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x3F, 16, 2);
🔧 Run I2C scanner (I can give if needed)
🔄 Rotate contrast screw
🔌 Check wiring again
⚠️ ABOUT LEDs & BUTTONS
You did right skipping them 👍

Without resistor:
LEDs → may burn ⚠️

Buttons → unstable readings

👉 So WAIT for resistors (don’t risk ESP32)

ok now tell me how to code on adrino as esp board is not showing

Alright — this is a setup issue, not a coding issue. Your ESP32 not showing in Arduino IDE is very common 👍
Follow this exactly and it will work.

⚙️ STEP 1: INSTALL ESP32 BOARD IN ARDUINO IDE
📌 Open Arduino IDE
Go to:

File → Preferences

Find:
👉 “Additional Board Manager URLs”

Paste this:

https://dl.espressif.com/dl/package_esp32_index.json
Click OK

📦 STEP 2: INSTALL ESP32 BOARDS
Go to:

👉 Tools → Board → Boards Manager

Search:

ESP32
Install:
👉 “ESP32 by Espressif Systems”

🔌 STEP 3: SELECT BOARD
After install:

👉 Tools → Board → ESP32 Arduino

Select:

ESP32 Dev Module (for your normal ESP32)

🔍 STEP 4: PORT NOT SHOWING (IMPORTANT)
Go to:
👉 Tools → Port

If NOTHING shows → problem here 👇
🧠 FIX: DRIVER ISSUE
If you are on Windows (likely):
Your ESP32 uses:

CP2102 or

CH340 driver

🔽 Install Drivers:
Option 1 (CP2102):
Search & install:
👉 “CP210x USB to UART driver”

Option 2 (CH340):
👉 “CH340 driver”

⚠️ After installing:
Restart Arduino IDE

Replug USB

Now check:
👉 Tools → Port → COMxx should appear

🔌 STEP 5: IF STILL NOT SHOWING
Try:

Different USB cable ⚠️ (very common issue)

Different USB port

Press BOOT button while uploading

🧪 STEP 6: TEST WITH BLINK CODE
Upload this:

void setup() {
  pinMode(2, OUTPUT);
}

void loop() {
  digitalWrite(2, HIGH);
  delay(1000);
  digitalWrite(2, LOW);
  delay(1000);
}
👉 LED on ESP32 should blink

⚠️ COMMON MISTAKES
❌ Using charge-only USB cable
❌ Not installing drivers
❌ Wrong board selected
❌ ESP32-CAM selected instead of ESP32

🚀 NEXT
Once:
👉 Port is visible
👉 Blink code works

Tell me:

👉 “esp working”

Then I’ll guide:

RTC code

LCD + RTC integration

Full medicine logic

We’ll build it clean step-by-step 💯


any other ide to code

Yes — you don’t have to stick to Arduino IDE. There are better options (especially if Arduino is giving problems). I’ll show you the best ones and tell you what I recommend for YOU 👇

🧠 BEST IDE OPTIONS FOR ESP32
🥇 1. Arduino IDE (Baseline)
Easiest for beginners

Tons of tutorials

Works with your current setup

👉 Problem: sometimes driver/port issues (what you faced)

✔️ Use this if you want quick and simple

🥈 2. PlatformIO (BEST CHOICE 🔥)
👉 This is what I strongly recommend for you

Why?
Works inside Visual Studio Code

Detects ESP32 better than Arduino

Handles libraries automatically

More professional + stable

🔧 How to install (simple):
Install VS Code

Open Extensions (left side)

Search:
👉 PlatformIO

Click Install

🚀 How to use:
Open PlatformIO

Click New Project

Select:

Board → ESP32 Dev Module

Framework → Arduino

Done ✅

🥉 3. ESP-IDF
Official framework from Espressif

Very powerful

BUT ❌ complicated for beginners

👉 Not recommended for your project right now

⚖️ WHAT YOU SHOULD DO (HONEST ADVICE)
If your goal = finish project FAST:
👉 Use Arduino IDE (fix driver issue)

If your goal = smooth experience + less errors:
👉 Use PlatformIO (BEST)

⚠️ IMPORTANT REALITY CHECK
Switching IDE won’t fix hardware problems like:

Bad USB cable

Missing drivers

Wrong board

👉 So even in PlatformIO, you may still need drivers

🚀 MY RECOMMENDATION FOR YOU
Since you’re building a full IoT project (not just small code):

👉 Go with:
✔️ PlatformIO + VS Code

It will help when you:

Add WiFi features

Build mobile app integration

Manage large code

👉 NEXT STEP
Tell me:

👉 “use platformio”
or
👉 “fix arduino”

I’ll guide you step-by-step setup (no confusion) and get your ESP running 💯

Perfect 👍 — that means your ESP32 + upload + port + drivers are all working. Now we move step-by-step like a proper system build.

🚀 NEXT STEP: LCD TEST (VERY IMPORTANT)
Now we confirm your display works, because it’s the main output for your project.

🔌 RECONFIRM CONNECTION (quick check)
LCD Pin	ESP32
VCC	5V
GND	GND
SDA	GPIO 21
SCL	GPIO 22
🧪 CLEAN WORKING CODE (USE THIS)
Replace your code with this:

#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>

// Try 0x27 first, if not working use 0x3F
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22); // Explicitly define I2C pins for ESP32
  
  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Initializing...");
}

void loop() {
}

🧪 STEP 1: SET TIME (RUN ONCE)
Upload this code ONLY ONCE to set RTC time:

#include <Wire.h>
#include <RTClib.h>

RTC_DS1307 rtc;

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  if (!rtc.begin()) {
    Serial.println("RTC not found");
    while (1);
  }

  rtc.adjust(DateTime(F(__DATE__), F(__TIME__))); // set current time
}

void loop() {
}
⚠️ IMPORTANT
Upload this ONCE

Then COMMENT or REMOVE rtc.adjust()
👉 otherwise time resets every upload

#include <RTClib.h>

RTC_DS1307 rtc;

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  rtc.begin();
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  Serial.print(now.hour());
  Serial.print(":");
  Serial.print(now.minute());
  Serial.print(":");

  delay(1000);

🚀 FULL WORKING CODE (CORE SYSTEM)
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;
Servo myServo;

#define buzzer 27

// SET YOUR MEDICINE TIME HERE
int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22);
  
  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);
  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  // Show time
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(now.hour());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.minute());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.second());

  // Check medicine time
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute) {
    
    lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
    lcd.print("TAKE MEDICINE!");

    digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);

    myServo.write(90); // dispense
    delay(3000);

    myServo.write(0);

    digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

    delay(60000); // avoid repeat
  }

  delay(1000);
}
🧠 WHAT THIS DOES
At your set time:

🔔 Buzzer rings

📺 LCD shows alert

🔁 Servo rotates → medicine drops

⚠️ IMPORTANT
👉 Change this:

int medMinute = XX;
Set it to 1–2 minutes ahead of current time for testing

We modify your main logic:

🔥 UPDATED FINAL LOGIC CODE
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;
Servo myServo;

#define buzzer 27
#define irPin 34

int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22);
  
  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);
  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(irPin, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(now.hour());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.minute());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.second());

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute) {

    lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    myServo.write(90); // dispense
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);

    // Wait for user to take medicine
    while (true) {
      int irValue = digitalRead(irPin);

      if (irValue == 0) {
        // Medicine taken
        digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
        lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
        lcd.print("Taken Thank You ");
        delay(3000);
        break;
      } else {
        // Not taken → keep alert
        digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
        lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
        lcd.print("Please Take Med ");
      }

      delay(500);
    }

    delay(60000); // prevent repeat
  }

  delay(1000);
}
🧠 WHAT YOU JUST BUILT
Now your system:

⏰ Tracks time

🔁 Dispenses medicine

🔔 Alerts user

👀 Detects if taken

🧠 Reacts intelligently

now tell me how 2 ir sensors are use to detect the object expain object like hand

Great question 👍 — this is exactly the kind of thing examiners ask.

Let’s make it clear + practical + viva-ready

👀 HOW IR SENSOR DETECTS OBJECT (like hand)
🧠 Working Principle
An IR module has:

IR LED (transmitter) → sends invisible infrared light

Photodiode (receiver) → receives reflected light

🔁 What happens:
👉 No object
IR light goes forward

Nothing reflects back

Sensor output = HIGH (1)

👉 Object present (like your hand)
IR light hits your hand

Light reflects back

Receiver detects it

Output = LOW (0)

📍 Visual idea

🧠 WHY USE 2 IR SENSORS?
Now comes the important logic for your project

🎯 PURPOSE IN YOUR PROJECT
You can use 2 sensors for better detection accuracy

🔹 METHOD 1: ENTRY + EXIT DETECTION (BEST)
Setup:
IR1 → near medicine outlet

IR2 → slightly below or further

🧠 Logic:
Situation	IR1	IR2	Meaning
No hand	1	1	Idle
Hand near	0	1	User approaching
Hand fully present	0	0	Taking medicine
Hand removed	1	1	Done
👉 This avoids false detection

🔹 METHOD 2: CONFIRMATION SYSTEM
IR1 → detects medicine dispensed

IR2 → detects user hand

Logic:
Servo drops medicine

IR1 detects pill passed

IR2 detects hand

👉 Only then mark: “medicine taken”

🔹 METHOD 3: POSITION DETECTION
IR1 → detect hand near

IR2 → detect hand moved away

👉 Helps confirm action completed

🧪 SIMPLE CODE FOR 2 IR SENSORS
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
  int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

  if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
    Serial.println("Hand Detected - Taking Medicine");
  }
  else if (s1 == 0) {
    Serial.println("Hand Near");
  }
  else {
    Serial.println("No Hand");
  }

  delay(500);
}
🧠 BEST WAY FOR YOUR PROJECT (RECOMMENDED)
👉 Use this logic:

Servo dispenses medicine

Start buzzer

Wait until:

IR1 detects object

AND IR2 detects object

Then:

Stop buzzer

Show “Medicine Taken”

⚠️ COMMON MISTAKES
❌ Sensors too far apart
❌ Not adjusting sensitivity knob
❌ Ambient light interference

You say:

but i thnk how light be refeclted from hand of ir its impossible i tired ;shloud both sensor shoul be facing each other

Good — you’re thinking correctly 👍 and also spotting a real-world problem, not just theory.

Let me correct something first:

👉 Reflection from hand is NOT impossible
BUT
👉 It is unreliable depending on distance, angle, and lighting

That’s why your test felt like “not working properly”

🧠 TRUTH ABOUT IR SENSORS (IMPORTANT)
These cheap IR modules are NOT perfect reflective sensors

They work best when:

Object is close (2–10 cm)

Surface reflects IR (hand works, but weak)

Angle is correct

❌ Why your hand test felt inconsistent
Skin absorbs some IR

Angle not correct

Distance too far

Sensitivity not tuned

👉 So yes, your doubt is valid 👍

🔥 SHOULD SENSORS FACE EACH OTHER?
✅ YES — THIS IS MUCH BETTER (BREAK-BEAM METHOD)
Instead of reflection, use:

👉 Beam interruption (most reliable)

🎯 HOW TO DO IT
Setup:
Place IR1 on one side

Place IR2 opposite side

Facing each other

So IR light travels like this:

IR1  ---> ---> ---> IR2
📍 When hand comes:
IR1  --->  ✋  ---> IR2 (blocked)
👉 Beam breaks → detection

use the break beam

Good choice 👍 — break-beam is much more reliable than reflection.

But I need to be very honest with you first (important):

⚠️ REALITY CHECK (VERY IMPORTANT)
👉 The IR modules you have are reflective sensors
❌ They are NOT true break-beam sensors

That means:

They don’t send beam to another module

Each module has its own transmitter + receiver

👉 So simply facing them at each other:
❌ will NOT work properly
❌ will give random results

🧠 THEN HOW TO DO “BREAK BEAM” WITH YOUR PARTS?
We can still simulate break-beam logic 🔥

✅ PRACTICAL SETUP (WORKS WITH YOUR COMPONENTS)
🎯 Placement (IMPORTANT)
Instead of facing directly:

👉 Place them like a gate / tunnel

   IR1        IR2
    |          |
    |          |
    |   ✋     |
    |          |
Both sensors facing same direction

Small gap between them (5–8 cm)

Hand passes through → both detect

🧠 LOGIC
We treat it like:

IR1	IR2	Meaning
1	1	No object
0	1	Entering
0	0	Inside (TAKEN)
1	1	Exit complete
👉 This simulates beam crossing

🔌 CONNECTION
Sensor	ESP32
IR1 OUT	GPIO 34
IR2 OUT	GPIO 35
VCC	3.3V
GND	GND
🔥 FINAL CODE (BREAK-BEAM LOGIC)
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

bool detected = false;

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
  int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

  // BOTH triggered → object inside
  if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0 && !detected) {
    Serial.println("Hand detected - Medicine Taken");
    detected = true;
  }

  // Reset after hand removed
  if (s1 == 1 && s2 == 1 && detected) {
    Serial.println("Ready for next detection");
    detected = false;
  }

  delay(200);
}
🧠 HOW THIS HELPS YOUR PROJECT
Now your system becomes:

Servo drops medicine

Wait for:

IR1 triggered

IR2 triggered

Then:

Stop buzzer

Show “Taken”

⚠️ TUNING (VERY IMPORTANT)
On both IR modules:

Rotate small blue knob

Set sensitivity so:

Hand → detected

No hand → not detected

❌ WHAT NOT TO DO
❌ Don’t place sensors too far
❌ Don’t face directly expecting laser beam
❌ Don’t skip calibration

🎓 VIVA GOLD ANSWER
If examiner asks:

👉 “How did you implement break beam?”

Say:

“True IR break-beam requires a dedicated transmitter and receiver, but due to hardware constraints, we simulated it using two reflective IR sensors placed in parallel. Detection occurs when both sensors simultaneously detect obstruction, ensuring reliable object confirmation.”

Good — but here’s the truth you need to know first 👇

👉 The potentiometer on IR module is NOT controlled by code ❌
👉 It is hardware tuning (manual screw adjustment) ✅

So you cannot “set it using code” — but I’ll help you tune it perfectly using code + testing 🔥

🧠 WHAT POTENTIOMETER DOES
That small blue screw adjusts:
👉 Sensitivity (distance detection threshold)

Turn one side → detects from far

Turn other side → detects only very close

🎯 BEST WAY TO ADJUST (WITH CODE)
We use Serial Monitor to see real-time detection

🧪 CALIBRATION CODE (USE THIS)
#define ir1 34

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  int val = digitalRead(ir1);

  if (val == 0) {
    Serial.println("DETECTED");
  } else {
    Serial.println("NO OBJECT");
  }

  delay(200);
}
🔧 STEP-BY-STEP ADJUSTMENT
1️⃣ Open Serial Monitor (115200)
You’ll see:

NO OBJECT
NO OBJECT
2️⃣ Put your hand where detection should happen
3️⃣ Slowly rotate potentiometer
👉 Use screwdriver
👉 Turn VERY slowly

🎯 GOAL
You want:

Condition	Output
No hand	NO OBJECT
Hand present	DETECTED
⚠️ IMPORTANT TUNING TIP
Stop when:
✔️ Detects ONLY when hand is close
❌ Not detecting randomly

🔥 FOR 2 IR SENSORS
Use this code:

#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  Serial.print("IR1: ");
  Serial.print(digitalRead(ir1));

  Serial.print(" | IR2: ");
  Serial.println(digitalRead(ir2));

  delay(200);
}
🎯 ADJUST BOTH SENSORS
Goal:

Both should give 0 when hand inside

Both should give 1 when empty

⚠️ COMMON PROBLEMS
❌ Always detecting → too sensitive → turn opposite
❌ Never detecting → increase sensitivity
❌ Random flicker → ambient light issue

🧠 PRO TIP (VERY IMPORTANT)
👉 Set detection distance to:
✔️ 3–6 cm only

This makes your project:

Accurate

Stable

Viva-friendly

Good question 👍 — and this is where many people get confused.

⚠️ IMPORTANT TRUTH
👉 With your IR module (digital type):

❌ You CANNOT measure distance in cm
❌ It only gives:

0 → object detected

1 → no object

👉 So it’s basically a switch, not a distance sensor

🧠 WHY?
Your module has:

Comparator circuit (LM393)

Potentiometer sets a threshold

👉 It doesn’t output distance
👉 It only tells: “object is within this range”

🎯 SO WHAT CAN YOU CONTROL?
👉 You control detection distance manually using potentiometer

Example:

Adjustment	Result
High sensitivity	Detects far (10–15 cm)
Low sensitivity	Detects near (2–5 cm)
🔧 HOW TO SET DESIRED DISTANCE (PRACTICAL)
🎯 Goal: Detect hand at ~5 cm
Steps:
Upload your code ✅

Open Serial Monitor

Keep hand at 5 cm distance

Slowly rotate potentiometer

👉 Stop when:

At 5 cm → DETECTED

At 10 cm → NO OBJECT

🧪 IMPROVED DEBUG CODE (BETTER VISUAL)
#define ir1 34

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
}

void loop() {
  int val = digitalRead(ir1);

  Serial.print("Sensor: ");
  Serial.print(val);

  if (val == 0) {
    Serial.println("  --> DETECTED");
  } else {
    Serial.println("  --> NO OBJECT");
  }

  delay(200);
}
🧠 THINK OF IT LIKE THIS
👉 Your IR sensor is like:

IF distance < threshold → DETECTED
ELSE → NOT DETECTED
👉 And threshold = set by potentiometer

🚀 IF YOU REALLY WANT DISTANCE
You would need:

Ultrasonic sensor (HC-SR04) ✅

OR IR analog distance sensor (Sharp GP2Y0A21)

🧠 FINAL WORKING LOGIC
Show time on LCD

🔥 FINAL CODE (COPY THIS)
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Set medicine time
int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  // Display time
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(now.hour());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.minute());
  lcd.print(":");
  lcd.print(now.second());

  // Check medicine time
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    // Dispense
    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);

    // Wait for detection
    while (true) {
      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
        lcd.clear();
        lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
        lcd.print("Medicine Taken");
        delay(3000);
        lcd.clear();
        break;
      } else {
        digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
        lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
        lcd.print("Please Take Med ");
      }

      delay(300);
    }
  }

  // Reset next day
  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}
⚠️ IMPORTANT SETTINGS
👉 Change this:

int medHour = XX;
int medMinute = XX;
Set it 1–2 minutes ahead for testing

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.print("Taken Thank You");

Perfect — now I’ll give you the FINAL STABLE + CLEAN + VIVA-READY CODE
👉 This includes ALL fixes we discussed:

✅ Clean LCD display
✅ Proper time format
✅ Servo control (stable)
✅ Buzzer beeping (not annoying)
✅ 2 IR sensors (with noise filtering)
✅ Timeout safety (very important)
✅ No repeated triggering

🔥 FINAL COMPLETE CODE (USE THIS)
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Set medicine time
int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  // Startup message
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  // Format time properly
  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   "); // clear extra chars

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  // Trigger condition
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    // Servo dispense
    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);

    // Timeout system (30 sec)
    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      // Noise filtering check
      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);
        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");
          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      // Buzzer beep (not continuous)
      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    // If not taken
    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");
      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  // Reset trigger after minute changes
  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}
⚠️ IMPORTANT SETTINGS
👉 Change this for testing:

int medHour = XX;
int medMinute = XX;
✔️ Set it 1–2 minutes ahead

🧠 WHAT MAKES THIS CODE “PRO LEVEL”
✅ No infinite loops

✅ Handles missed medicine

✅ Filters sensor noise

✅ Clean LCD output

✅ Controlled buzzer

✅ No repeated triggers

👉 This is project submission level code

📡 FINAL BLYNK CODE (MERGED WITH YOUR SYSTEM)
👉 Add WiFi + Blynk control:

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>

char auth[] = "YOUR_TOKEN";
char ssid[] = "YOUR_WIFI";
char pass[] = "YOUR_PASSWORD";

int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

// From app (Virtual Pin V0)
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}

// Manual button (V1)
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);
  }
}

void setup() {
  Blynk.begin(auth, ssid, pass);
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();
}

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "YOUR_TOKEN"

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>

#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "YOUR_WIFI";
char pass[] = "YOUR_PASSWORD";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 📱 BLYNK TIME INPUT
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}

// 📱 MANUAL BUTTON
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);
  }
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

        lcd.clear();
        lcd.print("Medicine Taken");
        delay(3000);
        break;
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Take Medicine  ");
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}
🧪 STEP 5: TESTING (VERY IMPORTANT)
1. Upload code
2. Open Serial Monitor
You should see:

Connecting to WiFi...
Connected
3. Open Blynk App
✔️ Press ▶️
✔️ Check device status → ONLINE

4. Test features

Press button	Servo rotates
Time match	Auto dispense

Check:

Same network

❌ Servo not moving
Check pin 13

Power issue

❌ Time not updating
Widget pin wrong

Not in run mode

Good — this is the most common Blynk issue, and it’s easy to fix once you understand it properly.

🚨 WHY YOUR DEVICE SHOWS “OFFLINE”
👉 In Blynk IoT
“Device Offline” = ESP32 has NOT connected to Blynk server

So the problem is ALWAYS one of these:

🔥 MAIN REASONS (CHECK THESE)
❌ 1. WiFi NOT added in code
👉 Important truth:

Blynk does NOT give WiFi name/password

👉 You must enter YOUR OWN WiFi details manually

📶 HOW TO GET WIFI NAME & PASSWORD
👉 On your phone:
Go to Settings → WiFi

See connected network name

Example:

SSID = Atharva_5G
👉 Password = the one you use to connect WiFi
(not shown in phone, you must know it)

❌ 2. WRONG WIFI TYPE
👉 ESP32 works BEST with:
✔️ 2.4 GHz WiFi

❌ Sometimes fails on:

5 GHz networks

❌ 3. WRONG AUTH TOKEN
👉 Must match EXACTLY from Blynk app

❌ 4. YOU DIDN’T UPLOAD UPDATED CODE
👉 After adding Blynk code → must upload again

void loop() {

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

Almost right — but one important correction 👇

👉 The USB cable is NOT used for Blynk connection ❌
👉 It is only used to upload code ✅

🧠 HOW IT ACTUALLY WORKS
After you upload the code, the connection is:

ESP32 → WiFi → Internet → Blynk Server → Blynk App
👉 NOT:

ESP32 → USB → Phone ❌
🔥 STEP-BY-STEP REAL FLOW
1️⃣ USB Cable (temporary use)
Connect ESP32 to laptop

Upload code from Arduino IDE

👉 That’s ALL USB does

2️⃣ After Upload (IMPORTANT)
ESP32 will:

Turn ON

Connect to your WiFi

Connect to Blynk IoT server

3️⃣ Your Phone
Your phone:

Also connects to internet

Talks to Blynk server

🧠 FINAL CONNECTION
PHONE APP ↔ INTERNET ↔ BLYNK SERVER ↔ ESP32
🎯 SIMPLE ANALOGY
ESP32 = worker

Blynk = boss

Internet = phone call

👉 USB is just “giving instructions once”

⚠️ IMPORTANT CONDITIONS
For it to work:

✔️ ESP32 must connect to WiFi
✔️ Phone must have internet
✔️ Token must match

❌ For your project:

👉 So:

🧠 PART 2 — HOW BLYNK CONNECTS (VERY IMPORTANT)
This is the core concept 🔥

🧩 THERE ARE 3 PARTS
1️⃣ Arduino IDE (your laptop)
👉 Used ONLY to:

Write code

Upload to ESP32

2️⃣ ESP32 (your hardware)
👉 Runs your code and connects to internet

3️⃣ Blynk App (your phone)
👉 Sends/receives data

🔥 ACTUAL CONNECTION FLOW
Arduino IDE → (USB) → ESP32
ESP32 → (WiFi) → Internet → Blynk Server
Phone App → (Internet) → Blynk Server
🧠 KEY POINT
👉 IDE is NOT connected to Blynk directly
👉 Only ESP32 talks to Blynk

🔑 WHAT LINKS EVERYTHING
👉 1. AUTH TOKEN (MOST IMPORTANT)
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "your_token"
👉 This tells server:

“this ESP32 = this device in app”

👉 2. WIFI DETAILS
char ssid[] = "your_wifi";
char pass[] = "your_password";
👉 This connects ESP32 to internet

👉 3. BLYNK CODE
Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);
Blynk.run();
👉 This connects ESP32 to Blynk server

🧠 FINAL UNDERSTANDING
👉 After upload:

ESP32 boots →
connects to WiFi →
connects to Blynk →
App becomes ONLINE
🧪 HOW YOU KNOW IT WORKS
In Serial Monitor:
Connected to WiFi
Connected to Blynk
In App:
✔️ Device = ONLINE

🚨 IF NOT CONNECTING
Then issue is always:

❌ Wrong token

❌ Wrong WiFi

❌ ESP32 not powered

🧠 SIMPLE ANALOGY
ESP32 = phone

Blynk = WhatsApp server

Token = phone number

👉 Without token → no connection

🚀 FINAL ANSWER
✔️ Ignore email setup
✔️ Your template is correct
✔️ IDE is only for uploading code
✔️ ESP32 + WiFi connects everything

kk now give me the full final code inlcluding everyhting 

Perfect — now I’ll give you the FINAL COMPLETE CODE
👉 Clean, stable, includes EVERYTHING:

📱 Blynk control

⏰ RTC timing

💊 Servo dispensing

🔔 Buzzer alert

👀 2 IR detection

📊 App status updates

💡 LED indicator (app side)

🔥 FINAL ALL-IN-ONE CODE
👉 Just replace:

TOKEN

WIFI

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "YOUR_TOKEN"

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "YOUR_WIFI";
char pass[] = "YOUR_PASSWORD";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

int medHour = 14;
int medMinute = 30;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 📱 TIME FROM APP
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 FUNCTION: DISPENSE
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);
  delay(3000);
  myServo.write(0);
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Waiting...");
  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

  // ⏰ TRIGGER TIME
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Take Medicine!");
    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 255);

    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      // 👀 Detection
      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Medicine Taken");
          Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      // 🔔 Buzzer beep
      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Take Medicine  ");
    }

    // ❌ Missed
    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.print("Missed Dose");

      Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Missed Dose");
      Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  // 🔁 Reset trigger
  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}
🧠 FINAL BLYNK SETUP (IMPORTANT)
Make sure your app has:

Feature	Pin
Time Input	V0
Button	V1
Status	V2
LED	V3
🧪 FINAL TEST CHECKLIST

#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Set medicine time
int medHour = 10;
int medMinute = 04;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

void setup() {
  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  // Startup message
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();
}

void loop() {
  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  // Format time properly
  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   "); // clear extra chars

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  // Trigger condition
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    // Servo dispense
    myServo.write(90);
    delay(3000);
    myServo.write(0);

    // Timeout system (30 sec)
    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      // Noise filtering check
      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);
        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");
          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      // Buzzer beep (not continuous)
      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    // If not taken
    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");
      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  // Reset trigger after minute changes
  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

Perfect — this is exactly what you needed 🔥

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "YOUR_TOKEN"

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "YOUR_WIFI";
char pass[] = "YOUR_PASSWORD";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Medicine time
int medHour = 10;
int medMinute = 4;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 📱 TIME FROM APP (V0)
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE (V1)
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 SERVO FUNCTION
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);
  delay(3000);
  myServo.write(0);
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  // Connect Blynk
  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  // Startup LCD
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  // Format time
  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   ");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Waiting...");
  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

  // ⏰ TRIGGER CONDITION
  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Take Medicine!");
    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 255);

    // Dispense
    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      // 👀 Detection with filtering
      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Medicine Taken");
          Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      // 🔔 Buzzer beep
      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    // ❌ Missed case
    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Missed Dose");
      Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  // Reset trigger
  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Medicine Taken");
          Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Missed Dose");
      Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}
👉 That means:

👉 Time widget often sends:

Either 1 value

Or timestamp

Or wrong format

🔥 FIX (VERY IMPORTANT)

BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  long t = param.asLong();

  medHour = hour(t);
  medMinute = minute(t);

  Serial.print("New Time Set: ");
  Serial.print(medHour);
  Serial.print(":");
  Serial.println(medMinute);
}

App sends timestamp

give the full code again #define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_ID "TMPL39IHNO8eS"
#define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_NAME "SMART MEDICINE DISPENSARY"
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU"

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "Asmit's F55";
char pass[] = "12345678";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Medicine time
int medHour = 10;
int medMinute = 4;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 📱 TIME FROM APP (V0)
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  medHour = param[0].asInt();
  medMinute = param[1].asInt();
}

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE (V1)
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 SERVO FUNCTION
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);
  delay(3000);
  myServo.write(0);
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  // Connect Blynk
  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  // Startup LCD
  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   ");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Waiting...");
  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Take Medicine!");
    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 255);

    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Medicine Taken");
          Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      Blynk.virtualWrite(V2, "Missed Dose");
      Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, 0);

      delay(3000);

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 SERVO FUNCTION
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);
  delay(3000);
  myServo.write(0);
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, "System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   ");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, "Waiting...");

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, "Take Medicine!");

    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, "Medicine Taken");

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, "Missed Dose");

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}
🧠 WHAT CHANGED
👉 Status moved:

V2 ❌ → V3 ✅
👉 Removed LED logic (since conflict)

📱 YOUR FINAL BLYNK SETUP
Widget	Pin
Time	V0
Button	V1
Status (Labelled Value)	V3
⚠️ IMPORTANT
In Labelled Value:

Value = /V3
🧪 RESULT
Now your app will show:

Waiting...

Medicine Taken

🔥 Final project polish
🔥 Viva explanation 💯

Blynk server sometimes ignores repeated same values

String lastStatus = "";

void updateStatus(String newStatus) {

    lastStatus = newStatus;
    Serial.println("Status: " + newStatus);
  }
}

updateStatus("Take Medicine!");

#define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_ID "TMPL39IHNO8eS"
#define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_NAME "SMART MEDICINE DISPENSARY"
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU"

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>
#include <TimeLib.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "Asmit's F55";
char pass[] = "12345678";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Medicine time
int medHour = 10;
int medMinute = 4;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 🔥 STATUS CONTROL
String lastStatus = "";

void updateStatus(String newStatus) {
  if (newStatus != lastStatus) {
    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, newStatus);
    lastStatus = newStatus;
    Serial.println("Status: " + newStatus);
  }
}

// 📱 TIME FROM APP
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  long t = param.asLong();

  medHour = hour(t);
  medMinute = minute(t);

  Serial.print("Time set: ");
  Serial.print(medHour);
  Serial.print(":");
  Serial.println(medMinute);
}

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 SERVO FUNCTION
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);
  delay(3000);
  myServo.write(0);
}

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  updateStatus("System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   ");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  updateStatus("Waiting...");

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    updateStatus("Take Medicine!");

    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          updateStatus("Medicine Taken");

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      updateStatus("Missed Dose");

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

🚨 ERROR EXPLAINED

Laptop ❌ cannot talk to ESP32
🔥 MOST COMMON FIX (WORKS 90% CASES)
👉 PRESS BOOT BUTTON METHOD
Do this exactly:
Click Upload in Arduino IDE

When you see:

Connecting....
👉 Press and HOLD BOOT button on ESP32

Release after 2–3 seconds

🧠 WHY THIS WORKS
ESP32 needs to go into:

FLASH MODE
👉 BOOT button forces that

🚀 IF STILL NOT WORKING
✅ CHECK 1: USB CABLE
👉 VERY common issue

Some cables = charging only ❌

Use data cable ✅

✅ CHECK 2: PORT
Go to:

Tools → Port
👉 Make sure:

COM7 (ESP32)
If not:

Replug USB

Try another port

✅ CHECK 3: BOARD SELECTED
Go to:

Tools → Board
👉 Select:

ESP32 Dev Module
✅ CHECK 4: DRIVER ISSUE (IMPORTANT)
If COM port unstable:

👉 Install:

CP210x driver OR

CH340 driver

(depending on your board)

✅ CHECK 5: CLOSE SERIAL MONITOR
👉 If Serial Monitor open:

Upload will FAIL ❌

👉 Not a problem

🚨 ISSUE 2 (IMPORTANT) — STATUS OVERRIDING
You are doing this:

updateStatus("Waiting...");
👉 every loop

🧠 WHAT HAPPENS
Even after:

updateStatus("Medicine Taken");
👉 It quickly becomes:

Waiting...
✅ FIX (SMART WAY)
Replace this:

updateStatus("Waiting...");
WITH:
if (!alreadyTriggered) {
  updateStatus("Waiting...");
}
⚠️ ISSUE 3 (MINOR BUT GOOD PRACTICE)
Inside this loop:

while (millis() - startTime < 30000)
👉 You are NOT running:

Blynk.run();
🧠 WHY THIS MATTERS
During 30 sec:

App becomes unresponsive ❌
✅ FIX
Add this inside loop:

while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

  Blynk.run();   // ⭐ ADD THIS

  int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
  int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);
🔥 FINAL FIX SUMMARY
✔ Fix 1:
Servo reset

myServo.write(0);
✔ Fix 2:
Prevent status override

if (!alreadyTriggered) {
  updateStatus("Waiting...");
}
✔ Fix 3:
Keep Blynk alive in loop

Blynk.run();

but i dont want reset servo as its rotating in direction only storing medi

Got it — and you’re thinking correctly 👍

👉 If your mechanism is:

One-direction rotation

Dispense happens only when rotating forward

No need to go back

👉 Then NOT resetting servo is perfectly valid ✅

🧠 BUT IMPORTANT CLARIFICATION
There are 2 types of servo setups:

🔹 CASE 1: NORMAL SG90 (most common)
👉 SG90 works like:

0° → left

90° → middle

180° → right

⚠️ It DOES NOT continuously rotate

👉 So if you leave it at 90:

It will STOP at 90 (not keep rotating)
🔹 CASE 2: CONTINUOUS SERVO (rare)
👉 Then:

90 = stop

0 = rotate one way

180 = rotate other way

🚨 YOUR CASE (MOST LIKELY)
You are using:
👉 SG90 (normal servo)

So your current logic:

myServo.write(90);
delay(3000);
👉 Means:

Rotate → reach position → STOP
🧠 WHAT THIS MEANS
👉 It is NOT continuously dispensing
👉 It is just moving to a position

🔥 BEST PRACTICE FOR MEDICINE DISPENSER
Even if you want “one direction” behavior:

👉 You SHOULD still:

myServo.write(90);
delay(3000);
myServo.write(0);
WHY?
Because:

Each trigger = one controlled cycle
Otherwise:

Next time → servo already at 90 → no movement ❌
⚠️ REAL ISSUE YOU MAY FACE
If you don’t reset:

👉 Next trigger:

Servo already at same angle → won't move → no dispensing ❌
🧠 ENGINEERING RECOMMENDATION
✅ KEEP RESET (BEST DESIGN)
myServo.write(90);
delay(3000);
myServo.write(0);
❌ ONLY REMOVE RESET IF:
✔ You are manually resetting
✔ Or using continuous servo
✔ Or mechanical return exists

🧠 SIMPLE ANALOGY
Think like:

👉 Button press → door opens
👉 If you never close → next press does nothing

🚀 FINAL ADVICE
👉 I strongly recommend:

✔ Keep reset
✔ Make dispensing repeatable

👉 NEXT

👉 “servo type: normal / continuous?”

I’ll guide you exactly based on your hardware so it becomes 100% reliable 💯

Good — now I’ll be very clear and honest so your system doesn’t fail later 👍

👉 Since you are using normal SG90, your current approach (no reset) is not reliable ❌

🚨 IMPORTANT REALITY (SG90 BEHAVIOR)
SG90 is position-based, not continuous.

0° → left  
90° → center  
180° → right  
👉 It moves once and stays there

⚠️ YOUR CURRENT LOGIC (NO RESET)
myServo.write(90);
delay(3000);
👉 First time:
✔ Servo moves → medicine drops

👉 Second time:
❌ Servo already at 90
❌ No movement
❌ No medicine

🧠 THAT MEANS
Your dispenser will:

Work only ONCE ❌
🔥 CORRECT ENGINEERING SOLUTION
You MUST create a cycle movement

✅ BEST WORKING CODE
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);   // open
  delay(2000);

  myServo.write(0);    // close (reset)
  delay(500);
}
🧠 WHY THIS IS REQUIRED
Because:

Each dose = one movement cycle
Without reset:

Next trigger = no motion = failure
⚙️ HOW REAL MEDICINE BOXES WORK
Even real systems:

✔ Rotate → dispense
✔ Return → ready for next dose

🧠 IF YOU WANT “ONE DIRECTION LOOK”
Then design like:

0° → slot closed  
90° → slot aligned → pill drops  
0° → back to block next pill  
👉 That’s how you simulate one-way dispensing

🚀 FINAL DECISION
Option	Result
No reset	❌ works only once
Reset (recommended)	✅ works every time
💯 FINAL ANSWER
👉 Since you are using SG90:

✔ You must reset servo
✔ Otherwise system will break after first use

#define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_ID "TMPL39IHNO8eS"
#define BLYNK_TEMPLATE_NAME "SMART MEDICINE DISPENSARY"
#define BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU"

#define BLYNK_PRINT Serial

#include <WiFi.h>
#include <BlynkSimpleEsp32.h>
#include <Wire.h>
#include <LiquidCrystal_I2C.h>
#include <RTClib.h>
#include <ESP32Servo.h>
#include <TimeLib.h>

// WiFi
char ssid[] = "Asmit's F55";
char pass[] = "12345678";

// LCD + RTC
LiquidCrystal_I2C lcd(0x27, 16, 2);
RTC_DS1307 rtc;

// Servo
Servo myServo;

// Pins
#define buzzer 27
#define ir1 34
#define ir2 35

// Medicine time
int medHour = 10;
int medMinute = 4;

bool alreadyTriggered = false;

// 🔥 STATUS CONTROL
String lastStatus = "";

void updateStatus(String newStatus) {
  if (newStatus != lastStatus) {
    Blynk.virtualWrite(V3, newStatus);
    lastStatus = newStatus;
    Serial.println("Status: " + newStatus);
  }
}

// 📱 TIME FROM APP
BLYNK_WRITE(V0) {
  long t = param.asLong();

  medHour = hour(t);
  medMinute = minute(t);

  Serial.print("Time set: ");
  Serial.print(medHour);
  Serial.print(":");
  Serial.println(medMinute);
}

// 📱 MANUAL DISPENSE
BLYNK_WRITE(V1) {
  if (param.asInt() == 1) {
    dispenseMedicine();
  }
}

// 🔧 SERVO FUNCTION
void dispenseMedicine() {
  myServo.write(90);   // open
  delay(2000);

  myServo.write(0);    // close (reset)
  delay(500);
}
void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);

  Wire.begin(21, 22);

  lcd.init();
  lcd.backlight();

  rtc.begin();

  myServo.attach(13);

  pinMode(buzzer, OUTPUT);
  pinMode(ir1, INPUT);
  pinMode(ir2, INPUT);

  Blynk.begin(BLYNK_AUTH_TOKEN, ssid, pass);

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Smart Med Box");
  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("System Ready");
  delay(2000);
  lcd.clear();

  updateStatus("System Ready");
}

void loop() {
  Blynk.run();

  DateTime now = rtc.now();

  char timeStr[9];
  sprintf(timeStr, "%02d:%02d:%02d", now.hour(), now.minute(), now.second());

  lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
  lcd.print("Time: ");
  lcd.print(timeStr);
  lcd.print("   ");

  lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
  lcd.print("Waiting...     ");

  updateStatus("Waiting...");

  if (now.hour() == medHour && now.minute() == medMinute && !alreadyTriggered) {

    alreadyTriggered = true;

    lcd.clear();
    lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
    lcd.print("Take Medicine!");

    updateStatus("Take Medicine!");

    dispenseMedicine();

    unsigned long startTime = millis();

    while (millis() - startTime < 30000) {

      int s1 = digitalRead(ir1);
      int s2 = digitalRead(ir2);

      if (s1 == 0 && s2 == 0) {
        delay(200);

        if (digitalRead(ir1) == 0 && digitalRead(ir2) == 0) {

          digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);

          lcd.clear();
          lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
          lcd.print("Medicine Taken");

          updateStatus("Medicine Taken");

          delay(3000);
          lcd.clear();
          break;
        }
      }

      digitalWrite(buzzer, HIGH);
      delay(200);
      digitalWrite(buzzer, LOW);
      delay(200);

      lcd.setCursor(0, 1);
      lcd.print("Please Take Med");
    }

    if (millis() - startTime >= 30000) {
      lcd.clear();
      lcd.setCursor(0, 0);
      lcd.print("Missed Dose!");

      updateStatus("Missed Dose");

      delay(3000);
      lcd.clear();
    }
  }

  if (now.minute() != medMinute) {
    alreadyTriggered = false;
  }

  delay(1000);
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Smart Medicine Box</title>
</head>

<body style="text-align:center; font-family:Arial;">

  <h1>Medicine Dispenser</h1>

  <button onclick="dispense()">Dispense Now</button>

  <br><br>

  <input type="time" id="timeInput">
  <button onclick="setTime()">Set Time</button>

  <script>
    const token = "YOUR_TOKEN";

    function dispense() {
      fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V1=1`);
    }

    function setTime() {
      let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;
      let [h, m] = t.split(":");

      let seconds = (h * 3600) + (m * 60);

      fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${seconds}`);
    }
  </script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
  const espIP = "http://192.168.1.100"; // CHANGE THIS

  function dispense() {
    fetch(`${espIP}/dispense`);
  }

  function setTime() {
    let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;
    let [h, m] = t.split(":");

    fetch(`${espIP}/setTime?h=${h}&m=${m}`);
  }

  function getStatus() {
    fetch(`${espIP}/status`)
      .then(res => res.text())
      .then(data => {
        document.getElementById("status").innerText = data;
      });
  }

  setInterval(getStatus, 2000);
</script>

</body>
</html>
🚀 PART 2 — ESP32 WEB SERVER CODE
👉 Add this inside your ESP32 code

🔥 ADD THESE LIBRARIES
#include <WiFi.h>
#include <WebServer.h>
🔥 CREATE SERVER
WebServer server(80);
🔥 ADD VARIABLES
String webStatus = "Waiting...";
🔥 ROUTES
void handleRoot() {
  server.send(200, "text/plain", "ESP32 Running");
}

void handleDispense() {
  dispenseMedicine();
  webStatus = "Manual Dispense";
  server.send(200, "text/plain", "Done");
}

void handleStatus() {
  server.send(200, "text/plain", webStatus);
}

void handleSetTime() {
  if (server.hasArg("h") && server.hasArg("m")) {
    medHour = server.arg("h").toInt();
    medMinute = server.arg("m").toInt();

    webStatus = "Time Updated";
  }
  server.send(200, "text/plain", "Time Set");
}
🔥 START SERVER IN SETUP
server.on("/", handleRoot);
server.on("/dispense", handleDispense);
server.on("/status", handleStatus);
server.on("/setTime", handleSetTime);

server.begin();
🔥 ADD THIS IN LOOP
server.handleClient();
🔥 UPDATE STATUS
Whenever you call:

updateStatus("Waiting...");
👉 ALSO DO:

webStatus = "Waiting...";

  function setTime() {
    let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;
    let [h, m] = t.split(":");

    let seconds = (h * 3600) + (m * 60);

    fetch(https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${seconds});

  function getStatus() {
  fetch(https://blynk.cloud/external/api/get?token=${token}&V3)
    .then(res => res.text())

      let el = document.getElementById("status");
      el.innerText = data;

      if (data.includes("Waiting")) el.style.color = "lightblue";
      else if (data.includes("Take")) el.style.color = "orange";
      else if (data.includes("Taken")) el.style.color = "green";
      else if (data.includes("Missed")) el.style.color = "red";

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Smart Medicine Dashboard</title>

  <style>
    body {
      font-family: Arial;
      background: #0f172a;
      color: white;
      text-align: center;
    }

      margin-top: 20px;
    }

      background: #1e293b;
      margin: 20px auto;
      padding: 20px;
      width: 320px;
      border-radius: 12px;
      box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);
      transition: 0.3s;
    }

    .card:hover {
      transform: scale(1.03);
    }

    button {
      background: #22c55e;
      border: none;
      padding: 10px 20px;
      color: white;
      border-radius: 6px;
      cursor: pointer;
      font-size: 16px;
    }

    button:hover {
      background: #16a34a;
    }

    input {
      padding: 10px;
      border-radius: 6px;
      border: none;
      font-size: 16px;
    }
  </style>

<body>

<h1>💊 Smart Medicine Dashboard</h1>

<!-- CLOCK -->
<div class="card">
  <h2>Current Time</h2>
  <p id="clock"></p>
</div>

<!-- STATUS -->
<div class="card">
  <h2>Status</h2>
  <p id="status" style="font-size:20px;">Loading...</p>
</div>

<!-- CONTROL -->
<div class="card">
  <h2>Manual Control</h2>
  <button onclick="dispense(event)">Dispense Now</button>
</div>

<!-- TIME -->
<div class="card">
  <h2>Set Medicine Time</h2>
  <input type="time" id="timeInput">
  <br><br>
  <button onclick="setTime()">Set Time</button>
</div>

<script>
  // 🔥 PUT YOUR TOKEN HERE
  const token = "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU";

  // 🕒 LIVE CLOCK
  setInterval(() => {
    let now = new Date();
    document.getElementById("clock").innerText =
      now.toLocaleTimeString();
  }, 1000);

  // 🔘 DISPENSE BUTTON
  function dispense(event) {
    let btn = event.target;
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerText = "Processing...";

    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V1=1`)
      .then(() => {
        setTimeout(() => {
          btn.disabled = false;
          btn.innerText = "Dispense Now";
        }, 3000);
      });
  }

  // ⏰ SET TIME
  function setTime() {
    let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;

    if (!t) {
      alert("Please select a time");
      return;
    }

    let [h, m] = t.split(":");
    let seconds = (h * 3600) + (m * 60);

    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${seconds}`)
      .then(() => {
        alert("Time set successfully!");
      });
  }

  // 📊 GET STATUS
  function getStatus() {
    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/get?token=${token}&V3`)
      .then(res => res.text())
      .then(data => {
        let el = document.getElementById("status");
        el.innerText = data;

        // 🎨 COLOR LOGIC
        if (data.includes("Waiting")) el.style.color = "lightblue";
        else if (data.includes("Take")) el.style.color = "orange";
        else if (data.includes("Taken")) el.style.color = "green";
        else if (data.includes("Missed")) el.style.color = "red";
        else el.style.color = "white";
      });
  }

  // 🔄 AUTO REFRESH
  getStatus();
  setInterval(getStatus, 2000);
</script>

</body>
</html>

Here’s a clear, structured, exam-ready + demo-ready summary of your entire project. You can use this for viva, report, presentation, or documentation.

💊 SMART MEDICINE DISPENSER SYSTEM
(IoT + Embedded + Web Integrated System)

🧠 1. PROJECT OVERVIEW
The Smart Medicine Dispenser is an IoT-based automated system that reminds users to take medicines on time, dispenses medication automatically, and monitors intake using sensors.

It provides:

⏰ Scheduled dispensing

📱 Mobile app control (Blynk)

🌐 Web dashboard control

🔔 Alerts and feedback

👀 Intake confirmation using sensors

🎯 2. OBJECTIVE
Ensure timely medication adherence

Reduce missed doses

Provide remote monitoring

Enable dual control system (App + Website)

⚙️ 3. SYSTEM ARCHITECTURE
        📱 Mobile App (Blynk)
                │
                ▼
          ☁️ Blynk Cloud
                │
                ▼
            ESP32 (Controller)
           /        |        \
      Servo     Sensors     Buzzer
       │           │           │
   Dispensing   Detection    Alert

                ▲
                │
        🌐 Website (API based)
🔧 4. HARDWARE COMPONENTS
Component	Function
ESP32	Main microcontroller (WiFi enabled)
DS1307 RTC	Real-time clock for scheduling
SG90 Servo	Controls medicine dispensing
IR Sensors (2)	Detect medicine pickup
Buzzer	Alerts user
LCD (16x2)	Displays status and time
Push Buttons	Manual interaction (optional)
💻 5. SOFTWARE COMPONENTS
Software	Purpose
Arduino IDE	Programming ESP32
Blynk IoT	Mobile app control
HTML/CSS/JS	Web dashboard
Blynk Cloud API	Communication between web and ESP32
🔁 6. WORKING PRINCIPLE
Step-by-step flow:
User sets medicine time via:

📱 Blynk app

🌐 Website

Time is stored in ESP32

RTC continuously tracks real time

When time matches:

Servo rotates → medicine dispensed

Buzzer alerts user

LCD + App shows: "Take Medicine!"

IR sensors detect if medicine is taken:

✔ If detected →

Status: "Medicine Taken"

❌ If not detected within 30 sec →

Status: "Missed Dose"

📱 7. MOBILE APP (BLYNK)
Features:
⏰ Set medicine time (V0)

🔘 Manual dispense button (V1)

📊 Live status display (V3)

Communication:
ESP32 ↔ Blynk Cloud ↔ Mobile App
🌐 8. WEBSITE DASHBOARD
Features:
💊 Dispense button

⏰ Time input

📊 Live status

🕒 Real-time clock

Communication:
Website → Blynk API → ESP32
🔔 9. ALERT SYSTEM
Buzzer activates during medicine time

Stops when:

Medicine is detected

OR timeout occurs

👀 10. SENSOR LOGIC
Two IR sensors ensure reliable detection:

Both sensors detect → Medicine taken
Else → Continue alert
🧠 11. STATUS SYSTEM
Condition	Status
Idle	Waiting...
Time reached	Take Medicine!
Detected	Medicine Taken
Timeout	Missed Dose
🔄 12. DATA FLOW
User Input → Cloud/API → ESP32 → Hardware Action
                                     ↓
                               Status Feedback
                                     ↓
                          App + Website Display
🔥 13. KEY FEATURES
✔ IoT-based remote control
✔ Dual interface (App + Website)
✔ Real-time monitoring
✔ Automatic dispensing
✔ Feedback system
✔ Sensor-based confirmation

🚀 14. ADVANTAGES
Reduces human error

Ensures timely medication

Remote monitoring possible

User-friendly interface

Scalable system

⚠️ 15. LIMITATIONS

Mechanical design dependency

<div class="grid">

  <!-- STATUS -->
  <div class="card">
    <h2>Status</h2>
    <div id="status" class="status">Loading...</div>
    <div id="connection" class="badge online">Online</div>
  </div>

  <!-- CLOCK -->
  <div class="card">
    <h2>Current Time</h2>
    <div id="clock" class="status"></div>
  </div>

  <!-- CONTROL -->
  <div class="card">
    <h2>Manual Control</h2>
    <button onclick="dispense(event)">Dispense Medicine</button>
  </div>

  <!-- TIMER -->

    <h2>Set Medicine Time</h2>
    <input type="time" id="timeInput">
    <button onclick="setTime()">Set Time</button>
  </div>

</div>

<script>
  const token = "YOUR_BLYNK_TOKEN";

  // CLOCK
  setInterval(() => {
    let now = new Date();
    document.getElementById("clock").innerText =
      now.toLocaleTimeString();
  }, 1000);

  // DISPENSE
  function dispense(event) {
    let btn = event.target;
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerText = "Processing...";

    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V1=1`)
      .then(() => {
        setTimeout(() => {
          btn.disabled = false;
          btn.innerText = "Dispense Medicine";
        }, 3000);
      });
  }

  // SET TIME
  function setTime() {
    let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;

    if (!t) {
      alert("Select time first");
      return;
    }

    let [h, m] = t.split(":");
    let seconds = (h * 3600) + (m * 60);

    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${seconds}`)
      .then(() => alert("Time Updated"));
  }

  // STATUS
  function getStatus() {
    fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/get?token=${token}&V3`)
      .then(res => res.text())
      .then(data => {
        let el = document.getElementById("status");
        el.innerText = data;

        if (data.includes("Waiting")) el.style.color = "#38bdf8";
        else if (data.includes("Take")) el.style.color = "#f59e0b";
        else if (data.includes("Taken")) el.style.color = "#22c55e";
        else if (data.includes("Missed")) el.style.color = "#ef4444";
      })
      .catch(() => {
        document.getElementById("connection").innerText = "Offline";
        document.getElementById("connection").className = "badge offline";
      });
  }

  getStatus();
  setInterval(getStatus, 2000);
</script>

</body>
</html>

📊 1. MEDICINE HISTORY (CHARTS)
🧠 HOW IT WORKS
We track:

✔ Medicine Taken

❌ Missed Dose

👉 Store it in browser (localStorage for now — simple & fast)

🔥 ADD THIS IN YOUR HTML (INSIDE GRID)
<div class="card">
  <h2>Medicine History</h2>
  <canvas id="chart"></canvas>
</div>
🔥 ADD CHART LIBRARY (TOP)
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
🔥 ADD THIS SCRIPT
let taken = localStorage.getItem("taken") || 0;
let missed = localStorage.getItem("missed") || 0;

const ctx = document.getElementById('chart');

let chart = new Chart(ctx, {
  type: 'doughnut',
  data: {
    labels: ['Taken', 'Missed'],
    datasets: [{
      data: [taken, missed],
      backgroundColor: ['#22c55e', '#ef4444']
    }]
  }
});

// Update history
function updateHistory(status) {
  if (status.includes("Taken")) {
    taken++;
    localStorage.setItem("taken", taken);
  }
  if (status.includes("Missed")) {
    missed++;
    localStorage.setItem("missed", missed);
  }

  chart.data.datasets[0].data = [taken, missed];
  chart.update();
}
🔥 MODIFY YOUR STATUS FUNCTION
Add this line inside getStatus():

updateHistory(data);

🔥 ADD JS FUNCTION
function showPopup(message, color) {
  let popup = document.getElementById("popup");
  let text = document.getElementById("popupText");

  text.innerText = message;
  popup.style.background = color;
  popup.style.display = "block";

  setTimeout(() => {
    popup.style.display = "none";
  }, 3000);
}
🔥 TRIGGER ALERTS
Inside getStatus():

if (data.includes("Take Medicine")) {
  showPopup("⏰ Time to take medicine!", "#f59e0b");
}

if (data.includes("Missed")) {
  showPopup("❌ Dose missed!", "#ef4444");
}

if (data.includes("Taken")) {
  showPopup("✅ Medicine taken!", "#22c55e");
}

<script>
  const token = "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU";

  // CLOCK
  setInterval(() => {
    let now = new Date();
    document.getElementById("clock").innerText =
      now.toLocaleTimeString();
  }, 1000);

  // DISPENSE
  function dispense(event) {
    let btn = event.target;
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerText = "Processing...";

    fetch(https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V1=1)
      .then(() => {
        setTimeout(() => {
          btn.disabled = false;
          btn.innerText = "Dispense Medicine";
        }, 3000);
      });
  }

  // SET TIME
  function setTime() {
    let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;

    if (!t) {
      alert("Select time first");
      return;
    }

    let [h, m] = t.split(":");
    let seconds = (h * 3600) + (m * 60);

    fetch(https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${seconds})
      .then(() => alert("Time Updated"));
  }

  // STATUS
  function getStatus() {
    fetch(https://blynk.cloud/external/api/get?token=${token}&V3)
      .then(res => res.text())
      .then(data => {
        let el = document.getElementById("status");
        el.innerText = data;

        if (data.includes("Waiting")) el.style.color = "#38bdf8";
        else if (data.includes("Take")) el.style.color = "#f59e0b";
        else if (data.includes("Taken")) el.style.color = "#22c55e";
        else if (data.includes("Missed")) el.style.color = "#ef4444";
      })
      .catch(() => {
        document.getElementById("connection").innerText = "Offline";
        document.getElementById("connection").className = "badge offline";
      });
  }

  getStatus();
  setInterval(getStatus, 2000);
</script>

</body>

<script>
const token = "9IZnV6T6HxYj6A4wMb6dM-aoUAo0J8eU";

// CLOCK
setInterval(() => {
  document.getElementById("clock").innerText =
    new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
}, 1000);

// DISPENSE
function dispense(event) {
  let btn = event.target;
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.innerText = "Processing...";

  fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V1=1`)
    .then(() => {
      setTimeout(() => {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.innerText = "Dispense Medicine";
      }, 3000);
    });
}

// SET TIME
function setTime() {
  let t = document.getElementById("timeInput").value;
  if (!t) return alert("Select time");

  let [h, m] = t.split(":");
  let sec = h*3600 + m*60;

  fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/update?token=${token}&V0=${sec}`)
    .then(()=> alert("Time Updated"));
}

// POPUP
function showPopup(msg, color) {
  let p = document.getElementById("popup");
  let t = document.getElementById("popupText");

  t.innerText = msg;
  p.style.background = color;
  p.style.display = "block";

  setTimeout(()=> p.style.display="none",3000);
}

// CHART
let taken = localStorage.getItem("taken") || 0;
let missed = localStorage.getItem("missed") || 0;

let chart = new Chart(document.getElementById("chart"), {
  type: 'doughnut',
  data: {
    labels: ['Taken','Missed'],
    datasets: [{
      data: [taken, missed],
      backgroundColor: ['#22c55e','#ef4444']
    }]
  }
});

// CAMERA
function loadCamera() {
  document.getElementById("cam").src =
    "http://192.168.1.101/capture?" + new Date().getTime(); // change IP
}

// STATUS TRACKING
let lastStatus = "";

function getStatus() {
  fetch(`https://blynk.cloud/external/api/get?token=${token}&V3`)
    .then(r=>r.text())
    .then(data=>{

      document.getElementById("status").innerText = data;

      // COLOR
      if(data.includes("Waiting")) color("#38bdf8");
      else if(data.includes("Take")) color("#f59e0b");
      else if(data.includes("Taken")) color("#22c55e");
      else if(data.includes("Missed")) color("#ef4444");

      // NEW STATUS ONLY
      if(data !== lastStatus){

        if(data.includes("Take")){
          showPopup("⏰ Time to take medicine","#f59e0b");
        }

        if(data.includes("Taken")){
          taken++;
          localStorage.setItem("taken",taken);
          showPopup("✅ Medicine Taken","#22c55e");
          loadCamera();
        }

        if(data.includes("Missed")){
          missed++;
          localStorage.setItem("missed",missed);
          showPopup("❌ Missed Dose","#ef4444");
        }

        chart.data.datasets[0].data = [taken, missed];
        chart.update();

        lastStatus = data;
      }
    })
    .catch(()=>{
      document.getElementById("connection").innerText="Offline";
      document.getElementById("connection").className="badge offline";
    });
}

function color(c){
  document.getElementById("status").style.color = c;
}

getStatus();
setInterval(getStatus,2000);
</script>

</body>
